\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{//    NO SECURITY GUARANTEE -\/-\/ DO NOT USE THIS ON UNTRUSTED FONT FILES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{// This library does no range checking of the offsets found in the file,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{// meaning an attacker can use it to read arbitrary memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{// =======================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{//   This library processes TrueType files:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{//        parse files}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{//        extract glyph metrics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{//        extract glyph shapes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{//        render glyphs to one-\/channel bitmaps with antialiasing (box filter)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{//        render glyphs to one-\/channel SDF bitmaps (signed-\/distance field/function)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{//   Todo:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{//        non-\/MS cmaps}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{//        crashproof on bad data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{//        hinting? (no longer patented)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{//        cleartype-\/style AA?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{//        optimize: use simple memory allocator for intermediates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{//        optimize: build edge-\/list directly from curves}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{//        optimize: rasterize directly from curves?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{96 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97 \textcolor{comment}{// USAGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{99 \textcolor{comment}{//   Include this file in whatever places need to refer to it. In ONE C/C++}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100 \textcolor{comment}{//   file, write:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{101 \textcolor{comment}{//      \#define STB\_TRUETYPE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 \textcolor{comment}{//   before the \#include of this file. This expands out the actual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{comment}{//   implementation into that C/C++ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 \textcolor{comment}{//   To make the implementation private to the file that generates the implementation,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106 \textcolor{comment}{//      \#define STBTT\_STATIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108 \textcolor{comment}{//   Simple 3D API (don't ship this, but it's fine for tools and quick start)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_BakeFontBitmap()               -\/-\/ bake a font to a bitmap for use as texture}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetBakedQuad()                 -\/-\/ compute quad to draw for a given char}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112 \textcolor{comment}{//   Improved 3D API (more shippable):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \textcolor{comment}{//           \#include "{}stb\_rect\_pack.h"{}           -\/-\/ optional, but you really want it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{114 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_PackBegin()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{115 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_PackSetOversampling()          -\/-\/ for improved quality on small fonts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{116 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_PackFontRanges()               -\/-\/ pack and renders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{117 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_PackEnd()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{118 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetPackedQuad()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{119 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{120 \textcolor{comment}{//   "{}Load"{} a font file from a memory buffer (you have to keep the buffer loaded)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{121 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_InitFont()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{122 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetFontOffsetForIndex()        -\/-\/ indexing for TTC font collections}}
\DoxyCodeLine{123 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetNumberOfFonts()             -\/-\/ number of fonts for TTC font collections}}
\DoxyCodeLine{124 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{125 \textcolor{comment}{//   Render a unicode codepoint to a bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{126 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetCodepointBitmap()           -\/-\/ allocates and returns a bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_MakeCodepointBitmap()          -\/-\/ renders into bitmap you provide}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetCodepointBitmapBox()        -\/-\/ how big the bitmap must be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{comment}{//   Character advance/positioning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetCodepointHMetrics()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetFontVMetrics()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetFontVMetricsOS2()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{comment}{//           stbtt\_GetCodepointKernAdvance()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{comment}{//   Starting with version 1.06, the rasterizer was replaced with a new,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 \textcolor{comment}{//   faster and generally-\/more-\/precise rasterizer. The new rasterizer more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{comment}{//   accurately measures pixel coverage for anti-\/aliasing, except in the case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 \textcolor{comment}{//   where multiple shapes overlap, in which case it overestimates the AA pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{//   coverage. Thus, anti-\/aliasing of intersecting shapes may look wrong. If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{//   this turns out to be a problem, you can re-\/enable the old rasterizer with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{comment}{//        \#define STBTT\_RASTERIZER\_VERSION 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 \textcolor{comment}{//   which will incur about a 15\% speed hit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{144 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{145 \textcolor{comment}{// ADDITIONAL DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{146 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{//   Immediately after this block comment are a series of sample programs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{149 \textcolor{comment}{//   After the sample programs is the "{}header file"{} section. This section}}
\DoxyCodeLine{150 \textcolor{comment}{//   includes documentation for each API function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{152 \textcolor{comment}{//   Some important concepts to understand to use this library:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{//      Codepoint}}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{comment}{//         Characters are defined by unicode codepoints, e.g. 65 is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{comment}{//         uppercase A, 231 is lowercase c with a cedilla, 0x7e30 is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{comment}{//         the hiragana for "{}ma"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 \textcolor{comment}{//      Glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{comment}{//         A visual character shape (every codepoint is rendered as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161 \textcolor{comment}{//         some glyph)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{162 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163 \textcolor{comment}{//      Glyph index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{164 \textcolor{comment}{//         A font-\/specific integer ID representing a glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{165 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{166 \textcolor{comment}{//      Baseline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{167 \textcolor{comment}{//         Glyph shapes are defined relative to a baseline, which is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{168 \textcolor{comment}{//         bottom of uppercase characters. Characters extend both above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169 \textcolor{comment}{//         and below the baseline.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{170 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{171 \textcolor{comment}{//      Current Point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{172 \textcolor{comment}{//         As you draw text to the screen, you keep track of a "{}current point"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{173 \textcolor{comment}{//         which is the origin of each character. The current point's vertical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{174 \textcolor{comment}{//         position is the baseline. Even "{}baked fonts"{} use this model.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{175 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{176 \textcolor{comment}{//      Vertical Font Metrics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{177 \textcolor{comment}{//         The vertical qualities of the font, used to vertically position}}
\DoxyCodeLine{178 \textcolor{comment}{//         and space the characters. See docs for stbtt\_GetFontVMetrics.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{180 \textcolor{comment}{//      Font Size in Pixels or Points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{181 \textcolor{comment}{//         The preferred interface for specifying font sizes in stb\_truetype}}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 \textcolor{comment}{//         is to specify how tall the font's vertical extent should be in pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{183 \textcolor{comment}{//         If that sounds good enough, skip the next paragraph.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{184 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{185 \textcolor{comment}{//         Most font APIs instead use "{}points"{}, which are a common typographic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{186 \textcolor{comment}{//         measurement for describing font size, defined as 72 points per inch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{187 \textcolor{comment}{//         stb\_truetype provides a point API for compatibility. However, true}}
\DoxyCodeLine{188 \textcolor{comment}{//         "{}per inch"{} conventions don't make much sense on computer displays}}
\DoxyCodeLine{189 \textcolor{comment}{//         since different monitors have different number of pixels per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{190 \textcolor{comment}{//         inch. For example, Windows traditionally uses a convention that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{191 \textcolor{comment}{//         there are 96 pixels per inch, thus making 'inch' measurements have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{192 \textcolor{comment}{//         nothing to do with inches, and thus effectively defining a point to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193 \textcolor{comment}{//         be 1.333 pixels. Additionally, the TrueType font data provides}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194 \textcolor{comment}{//         an explicit scale factor to scale a given font's glyphs to points,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{195 \textcolor{comment}{//         but the author has observed that this scale factor is often wrong}}
\DoxyCodeLine{196 \textcolor{comment}{//         for non-\/commercial fonts, thus making fonts scaled in points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{197 \textcolor{comment}{//         according to the TrueType spec incoherently sized in practice.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{198 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{199 \textcolor{comment}{// DETAILED USAGE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201 \textcolor{comment}{//  Scale:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202 \textcolor{comment}{//    Select how high you want the font to be, in points or pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203 \textcolor{comment}{//    Call ScaleForPixelHeight or ScaleForMappingEmToPixels to compute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204 \textcolor{comment}{//    a scale factor SF that will be used by all other functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{comment}{//  Baseline:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{comment}{//    You need to select a y-\/coordinate that is the baseline of where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{comment}{//    your text will appear. Call GetFontBoundingBox to get the baseline-\/relative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{//    bounding box for all characters. SF*-\/y0 will be the distance in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{//    that the worst-\/case character could extend above the baseline, so if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{//    you want the top edge of characters to appear at the top of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{comment}{//    screen where y=0, then you would set the baseline to SF*-\/y0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{comment}{//  Current point:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{//    Set the current point where the first character will appear. The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{comment}{//    first character could extend left of the current point; this is font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{//    dependent. You can either choose a current point that is the leftmost}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{//    point and hope, or add some padding, or check the bounding box or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{//    left-\/side-\/bearing of the first character to be displayed and set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{//    the current point based on that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{//  Displaying a character:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{//    Compute the bounding box of the character. It will contain signed values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{//    relative to <current\_point, baseline>. I.e. if it returns x0,y0,x1,y1,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{//    then the character should be displayed in the rectangle from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{//    <current\_point+SF*x0, baseline+SF*y0> to <current\_point+SF*x1,baseline+SF*y1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{//  Advancing for the next character:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{//    Call GlyphHMetrics, and compute 'current\_point += SF * advance'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{comment}{// ADVANCED USAGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{//   Quality:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Use the functions with Subpixel at the end to allow your characters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{comment}{//      to have subpixel positioning. Since the font is anti-\/aliased, not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{comment}{//      hinted, this is very import for quality. (This is not possible with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{comment}{//      baked fonts.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Kerning is now supported, and if you're supporting subpixel rendering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{comment}{//      then kerning is worth using to give your text a polished look.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{//   Performance:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Convert Unicode codepoints to glyph indexes and operate on the glyphs;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{comment}{//      if you don't do this, stb\_truetype is forced to do the conversion on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{comment}{//      every call.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ There are a lot of memory allocations. We should modify it to take}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{comment}{//      a temp buffer and allocate from the temp buffer (without freeing),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{comment}{//      should help performance a lot.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{255 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{comment}{//   The system uses the raw data found in the .ttf file without changing it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{257 \textcolor{comment}{//   and without building auxiliary data structures. This is a bit inefficient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{258 \textcolor{comment}{//   on little-\/endian systems (the data is big-\/endian), but assuming you're}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259 \textcolor{comment}{//   caching the bitmaps or glyph shapes this shouldn't be a big deal.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261 \textcolor{comment}{//   It appears to be very hard to programmatically determine what font a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262 \textcolor{comment}{//   given file is in a general way. I provide an API for this, but I don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263 \textcolor{comment}{//   recommend it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{265 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{266 \textcolor{comment}{// PERFORMANCE MEASUREMENTS FOR 1.06:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{267 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{268 \textcolor{comment}{//                      32-\/bit     64-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{269 \textcolor{comment}{//   Previous release:  8.83 s     7.68 s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{270 \textcolor{comment}{//   Pool allocations:  7.72 s     6.34 s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{271 \textcolor{comment}{//   Inline sort     :  6.54 s     5.65 s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{272 \textcolor{comment}{//   New rasterizer  :  5.63 s     5.00 s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{273 }
\DoxyCodeLine{279 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \textcolor{comment}{//  Incomplete text-\/in-\/3d-\/api example, which draws quads properly aligned to be lossless.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{comment}{//  See "{}tests/truetype\_demo\_win32.c"{} for a complete version.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{282 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{283 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STB\_TRUETYPE\_IMPLEMENTATION  }\textcolor{comment}{// force following include to generate implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{284 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include "{}stb\_truetype.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{285 }
\DoxyCodeLine{286 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} ttf\_buffer[1<<20];}
\DoxyCodeLine{287 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} temp\_bitmap[512*512];}
\DoxyCodeLine{288 }
\DoxyCodeLine{289 \mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__bakedchar}{stbtt\_bakedchar}} cdata[96]; \textcolor{comment}{// ASCII 32..126 is 95 glyphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{290 GLuint ftex;}
\DoxyCodeLine{291 }

\DoxyCodeLine{620 \textcolor{comment}{// and pass that result as 'font\_size':}}
\DoxyCodeLine{621 \textcolor{comment}{//       ...,                  20 , ... // font max minus min y is 20 pixels tall}}
\DoxyCodeLine{622 \textcolor{comment}{//       ..., STBTT\_POINT\_SIZE(20), ... // 'M' is 20 pixels tall}}

\DoxyCodeLine{640 \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_ab459250c5579b1d942e0d8eb23936827}{STBTT\_DEF}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_a4c55e174efbacaf82a8ddb9d1956717e}{stbtt\_PackSetOversampling}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__pack__context}{stbtt\_pack\_context}} *spc, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h\_oversample, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} v\_oversample);}
\DoxyCodeLine{641 \textcolor{comment}{// Oversampling a font increases the quality by allowing higher-\/quality subpixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{642 \textcolor{comment}{// positioning, and is especially valuable at smaller text sizes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{643 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{644 \textcolor{comment}{// This function sets the amount of oversampling for all following calls to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{645 \textcolor{comment}{// stbtt\_PackFontRange(s) or stbtt\_PackFontRangesGatherRects for a given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{646 \textcolor{comment}{// pack context. The default (no oversampling) is achieved by h\_oversample=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{647 \textcolor{comment}{// and v\_oversample=1. The total number of pixels required is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{648 \textcolor{comment}{// h\_oversample*v\_oversample larger than the default; for example, 2x2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{649 \textcolor{comment}{// oversampling requires 4x the storage of 1x1. For best results, render}}
\DoxyCodeLine{650 \textcolor{comment}{// oversampled textures with bilinear filtering. Look at the readme in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{651 \textcolor{comment}{// stb/tests/oversample for information about oversampled fonts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{652 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{653 \textcolor{comment}{// To use with PackFontRangesGather etc., you must set it before calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{654 \textcolor{comment}{// call to PackFontRangesGatherRects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{655 }

\DoxyCodeLine{764 \textcolor{comment}{// computes a scale factor to produce a font whose "{}height"{} is 'pixels' tall.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{768 \textcolor{comment}{//       scale = pixels / (ascent -\/ descent)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{935 \textcolor{comment}{// rasterize a shape with quadratic beziers into a bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{936 \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_ab459250c5579b1d942e0d8eb23936827}{STBTT\_DEF}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_a5b868ef9a9f92e0cc8b6bc0dd52087db}{stbtt\_Rasterize}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt____bitmap}{stbtt\_\_bitmap}} *result,        \textcolor{comment}{// 1-\/channel bitmap to draw into}}

\DoxyCodeLine{945 }
\DoxyCodeLine{947 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{948 \textcolor{comment}{// Signed Distance Function (or Field) rendering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{949 }
\DoxyCodeLine{950 \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_ab459250c5579b1d942e0d8eb23936827}{STBTT\_DEF}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_a1254dc807df81931ab070c6e80370489}{stbtt\_FreeSDF}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *bitmap, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *userdata);}
\DoxyCodeLine{951 \textcolor{comment}{// frees the SDF bitmap allocated below}}
\DoxyCodeLine{952 }
\DoxyCodeLine{953 \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_ab459250c5579b1d942e0d8eb23936827}{STBTT\_DEF}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} * \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_a86f324094c416b920f5a4df75b3abe97}{stbtt\_GetGlyphSDF}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__fontinfo}{stbtt\_fontinfo}} *info, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} scale, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} glyph, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} padding, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} onedge\_value, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} pixel\_dist\_scale, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *xoff, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *yoff);}
\DoxyCodeLine{954 \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_ab459250c5579b1d942e0d8eb23936827}{STBTT\_DEF}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} * \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_ae70e9e09a74359133d5f282e032d5aa7}{stbtt\_GetCodepointSDF}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__fontinfo}{stbtt\_fontinfo}} *info, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} scale, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} codepoint, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} padding, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} onedge\_value, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} pixel\_dist\_scale, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *xoff, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *yoff);}
\DoxyCodeLine{955 \textcolor{comment}{// These functions compute a discretized SDF field for a single character, suitable for storing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{956 \textcolor{comment}{// in a single-\/channel texture, sampling with bilinear filtering, and testing against}}
\DoxyCodeLine{957 \textcolor{comment}{// larger than some threshold to produce scalable fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{958 \textcolor{comment}{//        info              -\/-\/  the font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{959 \textcolor{comment}{//        scale             -\/-\/  controls the size of the resulting SDF bitmap, same as it would be creating a regular bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{960 \textcolor{comment}{//        glyph/codepoint   -\/-\/  the character to generate the SDF for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{961 \textcolor{comment}{//        padding           -\/-\/  extra "{}pixels"{} around the character which are filled with the distance to the character (not 0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{962 \textcolor{comment}{//                                 which allows effects like bit outlines}}
\DoxyCodeLine{963 \textcolor{comment}{//        onedge\_value      -\/-\/  value 0-\/255 to test the SDF against to reconstruct the character (i.e. the isocontour of the character)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{964 \textcolor{comment}{//        pixel\_dist\_scale  -\/-\/  what value the SDF should increase by when moving one SDF "{}pixel"{} away from the edge (on the 0..255 scale)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{965 \textcolor{comment}{//                                 if positive, > onedge\_value is inside; if negative, < onedge\_value is inside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{966 \textcolor{comment}{//        width,height      -\/-\/  output height \& width of the SDF bitmap (including padding)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{967 \textcolor{comment}{//        xoff,yoff         -\/-\/  output origin of the character}}
\DoxyCodeLine{968 \textcolor{comment}{//        return value      -\/-\/  a 2D array of bytes 0..255, width*height in size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{969 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{970 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel\_dist\_scale \& onedge\_value are a scale \& bias that allows you to make}}
\DoxyCodeLine{971 \textcolor{comment}{// optimal use of the limited 0..255 for your application, trading off precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{972 \textcolor{comment}{// and special effects. SDF values outside the range 0..255 are clamped to 0..255.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{973 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{974 \textcolor{comment}{// Example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{975 \textcolor{comment}{//      scale = stbtt\_ScaleForPixelHeight(22)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{976 \textcolor{comment}{//      padding = 5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{977 \textcolor{comment}{//      onedge\_value = 180}}
\DoxyCodeLine{978 \textcolor{comment}{//      pixel\_dist\_scale = 180/5.0 = 36.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{979 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{980 \textcolor{comment}{//      This will create an SDF bitmap in which the character is about 22 pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{981 \textcolor{comment}{//      high but the whole bitmap is about 22+5+5=32 pixels high. To produce a filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{982 \textcolor{comment}{//      shape, sample the SDF at each pixel and fill the pixel if the SDF value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{983 \textcolor{comment}{//      is greater than or equal to 180/255. (You'll actually want to antialias,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{984 \textcolor{comment}{//      which is beyond the scope of this example.) Additionally, you can compute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{985 \textcolor{comment}{//      offset outlines (e.g. to stroke the character border inside \& outside,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{986 \textcolor{comment}{//      or only outside). For example, to fill outside the character up to 3 SDF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{987 \textcolor{comment}{//      pixels, you would compare against (180-\/36.0*3)/255 = 72/255. The above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{988 \textcolor{comment}{//      choice of variables maps a range from 5 pixels outside the shape to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{989 \textcolor{comment}{//      2 pixels inside the shape to 0..255; this is intended primarily for apply}}
\DoxyCodeLine{990 \textcolor{comment}{//      outside effects only (the interior range is needed to allow proper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{991 \textcolor{comment}{//      antialiasing of the font at *smaller* sizes)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{992 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{993 \textcolor{comment}{// The function computes the SDF analytically at each SDF pixel, not by e.g.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{994 \textcolor{comment}{// building a higher-\/res bitmap and approximating it. In theory the quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{995 \textcolor{comment}{// should be as high as possible for an SDF of this size \& representation, but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{996 \textcolor{comment}{// unclear if this is true in practice (perhaps building a higher-\/res bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{997 \textcolor{comment}{// and computing from that can allow drop-\/out prevention).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{998 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{999 \textcolor{comment}{// The algorithm has not been optimized at all, so expect it to be slow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1000 \textcolor{comment}{// if computing lots of characters or very large sizes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1001 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1002 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1003 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1005 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1006 \textcolor{comment}{// Finding the right font...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1007 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1008 \textcolor{comment}{// You should really just solve this offline, keep your own tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1009 \textcolor{comment}{// of what font is what, and don't try to get it out of the .ttf file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1010 \textcolor{comment}{// That's because getting it out of the .ttf file is really hard, because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1011 \textcolor{comment}{// the names in the file can appear in many possible encodings, in many}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1012 \textcolor{comment}{// possible languages, and e.g. if you need a case-\/insensitive comparison,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1013 \textcolor{comment}{// the details of that depend on the encoding \& language in a complex way}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1014 \textcolor{comment}{// (actually underspecified in truetype, but also gigantic).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1015 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1016 \textcolor{comment}{// But you can use the provided functions in two possible ways:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1017 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbtt\_FindMatchingFont() will use *case-\/sensitive* comparisons on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1018 \textcolor{comment}{//             unicode-\/encoded names to try to find the font you want;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1019 \textcolor{comment}{//             you can run this before calling stbtt\_InitFont()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1020 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1021 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbtt\_GetFontNameString() lets you get any of the various strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1022 \textcolor{comment}{//             from the file yourself and do your own comparisons on them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1023 \textcolor{comment}{//             You have to have called stbtt\_InitFont() first.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1024 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1025 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1026 \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_ab459250c5579b1d942e0d8eb23936827}{STBTT\_DEF}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_a76ec14e5c7e57981dc5a409d89b5e92f}{stbtt\_FindMatchingFont}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *fontdata, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *name, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} flags);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1027 \textcolor{comment}{// returns the offset (not index) of the font that matches, or -\/1 if none}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1028 \textcolor{comment}{//   if you use STBTT\_MACSTYLE\_DONTCARE, use a font name like "{}Arial Bold"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1029 \textcolor{comment}{//   if you use any other flag, use a font name like "{}Arial"{}; this checks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1030 \textcolor{comment}{//     the 'macStyle' header field; i don't know if fonts set this consistently}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1031 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBTT\_MACSTYLE\_DONTCARE     0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1032 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBTT\_MACSTYLE\_BOLD         1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1033 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBTT\_MACSTYLE\_ITALIC       2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1034 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBTT\_MACSTYLE\_UNDERSCORE   4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1035 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBTT\_MACSTYLE\_NONE         8   }\textcolor{comment}{// <= not same as 0, this makes us check the bitfield is 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1036 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1037 \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_ab459250c5579b1d942e0d8eb23936827}{STBTT\_DEF}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \mbox{\hyperlink{imstb__truetype_8h_aafc4974ee424f18246f47b0926a1cd31}{stbtt\_CompareUTF8toUTF16\_bigendian}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *s1, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len1, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *s2, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1038 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1/0 whether the first string interpreted as utf8 is identical to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2883 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if STBTT\_RASTERIZER\_VERSION == 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2884 \textcolor{comment}{// note: this routine clips fills that extend off the edges... ideally this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2885 \textcolor{comment}{// wouldn't happen, but it could happen if the truetype glyph bounding boxes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2886 \textcolor{comment}{// are wrong, or if the user supplies a too-\/small bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2887 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbtt\_\_fill\_active\_edges(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *scanline, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len, stbtt\_\_active\_edge *e, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} max\_weight)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2888 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2889    \textcolor{comment}{// non-\/zero winding fill}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2890    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x0=0, w=0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2891 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2892    \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (e) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2893       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2894          \textcolor{comment}{// if we're currently at zero, we need to record the edge start point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2895          x0 = e-\/>x; w += e-\/>direction;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2896       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2897          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x1 = e-\/>x; w += e-\/>direction;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2898          \textcolor{comment}{// if we went to zero, we need to draw}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2899          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2900             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = x0 >> STBTT\_FIXSHIFT;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2901             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} j = x1 >> STBTT\_FIXSHIFT;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2902 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2903             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i < len \&\& j >= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2904                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i == j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2905                   \textcolor{comment}{// x0,x1 are the same pixel, so compute combined coverage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2906                   scanline[i] = scanline[i] + (stbtt\_uint8) ((x1 -\/ x0) * max\_weight >> STBTT\_FIXSHIFT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2907                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2908                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i >= 0) \textcolor{comment}{// add antialiasing for x0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2909                      scanline[i] = scanline[i] + (stbtt\_uint8) (((STBTT\_FIX -\/ (x0 \& STBTT\_FIXMASK)) * max\_weight) >> STBTT\_FIXSHIFT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2910                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2911                      i = -\/1; \textcolor{comment}{// clip}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2913                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j < len) \textcolor{comment}{// add antialiasing for x1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914                      scanline[j] = scanline[j] + (stbtt\_uint8) (((x1 \& STBTT\_FIXMASK) * max\_weight) >> STBTT\_FIXSHIFT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916                      j = len; \textcolor{comment}{// clip}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2917 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2918                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (++i; i < j; ++i) \textcolor{comment}{// fill pixels between x0 and x1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919                      scanline[i] = scanline[i] + (stbtt\_uint8) max\_weight;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2920                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2921             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2922          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2923       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2924 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2925       e = e-\/>next;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2926    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2927 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2928 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2929 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbtt\_\_rasterize\_sorted\_edges(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt____bitmap}{stbtt\_\_bitmap}} *result, stbtt\_\_edge *e, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} vsubsample, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} off\_x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} off\_y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *userdata)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2950          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} scan\_y = y + 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2951          stbtt\_\_active\_edge **step = \&active;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2952 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2953          \textcolor{comment}{// update all active edges;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2954          \textcolor{comment}{// remove all active edges that terminate before the center of this scanline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2955          \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (*step) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2956             stbtt\_\_active\_edge * z = *step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2957             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>ey <= scan\_y) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2958                *step = z-\/>next; \textcolor{comment}{// delete from list}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2964                step = \&((*step)-\/>next); \textcolor{comment}{// advance through list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2965             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2966          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2967 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2968          \textcolor{comment}{// resort the list if needed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2969          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(;;) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2970             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} changed=0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2971             step = \&active;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2973                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((*step)-\/>x > (*step)-\/>next-\/>x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2974                   stbtt\_\_active\_edge *t = *step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2975                   stbtt\_\_active\_edge *q = t-\/>next;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2976 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2977                   t-\/>next = q-\/>next;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2978                   q-\/>next = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2979                   *step = q;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2980                   changed = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2981                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2982                step = \&(*step)-\/>next;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2983             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2984             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!changed) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2985          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2986 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2987          \textcolor{comment}{// insert all edges that start before the center of this scanline -\/-\/ omit ones that also end on this scanline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2988          \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (e-\/>y0 <= scan\_y) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2989             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (e-\/>y1 > scan\_y) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2990                stbtt\_\_active\_edge *z = stbtt\_\_new\_active(\&hh, e, off\_x, scan\_y, userdata);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2991                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z != NULL) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2992                   \textcolor{comment}{// find insertion point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2993                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (active == NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2994                      active = z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2995                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>x < active-\/>x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2996                      \textcolor{comment}{// insert at front}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2997                      z-\/>next = active;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2998                      active = z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2999                   \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3000                      \textcolor{comment}{// find thing to insert AFTER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3001                      stbtt\_\_active\_edge *p = active;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3002                      \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (p-\/>next \&\& p-\/>next-\/>x < z-\/>x)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3003                         p = p-\/>next;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3004                      \textcolor{comment}{// at this point, p-\/>next-\/>x is NOT < z-\/>x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3005                      z-\/>next = p-\/>next;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3006                      p-\/>next = z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3007                   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3008                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3009             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3010             ++e;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3011          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3012 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3013          \textcolor{comment}{// now process all active edges in XOR fashion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3014          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (active)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3015             stbtt\_\_fill\_active\_edges(scanline, result-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt____bitmap_afbd607426f0a457b1a871ed902eeb926}{w}}, active, max\_weight);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3016 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3017          ++y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3018       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3019       STBTT\_memcpy(result-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt____bitmap_ae6be77625faf55b110eaaffde5c7733c}{pixels}} + j * result-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt____bitmap_a48ee6b550ee4f1d85bfc32c62c0e9a98}{stride}}, scanline, result-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt____bitmap_afbd607426f0a457b1a871ed902eeb926}{w}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3020       ++j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3021    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3022 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3023    stbtt\_\_hheap\_cleanup(\&hh, userdata);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3024 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3025    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (scanline != scanline\_data)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3026       \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a357d3564409e68f1b694e06f7beeca7e}{STBTT\_free}}(scanline, userdata);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3027 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3028 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3029 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif STBTT\_RASTERIZER\_VERSION == 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3030 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3031 \textcolor{comment}{// the edge passed in here does not cross the vertical line at x or the vertical line at x+1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3032 \textcolor{comment}{// (i.e. it has already been clipped to those)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3033 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} *scanline, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x, stbtt\_\_active\_edge *e, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x1, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3034 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3035    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (y0 == y1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3036    \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(y0 < y1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3037    \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(e-\/>sy <= e-\/>ey);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3039    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (y1 < e-\/>sy) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}

\DoxyCodeLine{3043    \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3046       y1 = e-\/>ey;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3047    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3048 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3049    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 == x)}

\DoxyCodeLine{3051    \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 == x+1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3052       \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(x1 >= x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3053    \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 <= x)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3054       \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(x1 <= x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3055    \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 >= x+1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3056       \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(x1 >= x+1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3057    \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3058       \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(x1 >= x \&\& x1 <= x+1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3059 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3060    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 <= x \&\& x1 <= x)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3061       scanline[x] += e-\/>direction * (y1-\/y0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3062    \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 >= x+1 \&\& x1 >= x+1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3063       ;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3064    \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3065       \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(x0 >= x \&\& x0 <= x+1 \&\& x1 >= x \&\& x1 <= x+1);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3067    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3068 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3069 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3070 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} stbtt\_\_sized\_trapezoid\_area(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} top\_width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} bottom\_width)}

\DoxyCodeLine{3086 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3087 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbtt\_\_fill\_active\_edges\_new(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} *scanline, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} *scanline\_fill, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len, stbtt\_\_active\_edge *e, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y\_top)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3088 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3089    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y\_bottom = y\_top+1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3090 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3091    \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (e) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3092       \textcolor{comment}{// brute force every pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3093 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3094       \textcolor{comment}{// compute intersection points with top \& bottom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3095       \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(e-\/>ey >= y\_top);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3097       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (e-\/>fdx == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3098          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x0 = e-\/>fx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3099          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 < len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3100             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 >= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3101                stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}) x0,e, x0,y\_top, x0,y\_bottom);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3102                stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline\_fill-\/1,(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}) x0+1,e, x0,y\_top, x0,y\_bottom);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3103             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3104                stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline\_fill-\/1,0,e, x0,y\_top, x0,y\_bottom);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3105             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3106          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3107       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3108          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x0 = e-\/>fx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3109          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} dx = e-\/>fdx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3110          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} xb = x0 + dx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3111          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x\_top, x\_bottom;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3112          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} sy0,sy1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3113          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} dy = e-\/>fdy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3114          \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(e-\/>sy <= y\_bottom \&\& e-\/>ey >= y\_top);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3115 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3116          \textcolor{comment}{// compute endpoints of line segment clipped to this scanline (if the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3117          \textcolor{comment}{// line segment starts on this scanline. x0 is the intersection of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3118          \textcolor{comment}{// line with y\_top, but that may be off the line segment.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3119          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (e-\/>sy > y\_top) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3120             x\_top = x0 + dx * (e-\/>sy -\/ y\_top);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3121             sy0 = e-\/>sy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3122          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3123             x\_top = x0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3124             sy0 = y\_top;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3125          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3126          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (e-\/>ey < y\_bottom) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3127             x\_bottom = x0 + dx * (e-\/>ey -\/ y\_top);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3128             sy1 = e-\/>ey;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3129          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3130             x\_bottom = xb;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3131             sy1 = y\_bottom;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3132          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3133 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3134          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x\_top >= 0 \&\& x\_bottom >= 0 \&\& x\_top < len \&\& x\_bottom < len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3135             \textcolor{comment}{// from here on, we don't have to range check x values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3136 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3137             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}) x\_top == (int) x\_bottom) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3138                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3139                \textcolor{comment}{// simple case, only spans one pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3140                \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x = (int) x\_top;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3141                height = (sy1 -\/ sy0) * e-\/>direction;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3142                \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(x >= 0 \&\& x < len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3143                scanline[x]      += stbtt\_\_position\_trapezoid\_area(height, x\_top, x+1.0f, x\_bottom, x+1.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3144                scanline\_fill[x] += height; \textcolor{comment}{// everything right of this pixel is filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3145             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3146                \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x,x1,x2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3147                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y\_crossing, y\_final, step, sign, area;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3148                \textcolor{comment}{// covers 2+ pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3149                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x\_top > x\_bottom) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3150                   \textcolor{comment}{// flip scanline vertically; signed area is the same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3151                   \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3152                   sy0 = y\_bottom -\/ (sy0 -\/ y\_top);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3153                   sy1 = y\_bottom -\/ (sy1 -\/ y\_top);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3154                   t = sy0, sy0 = sy1, sy1 = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3155                   t = x\_bottom, x\_bottom = x\_top, x\_top = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3156                   dx = -\/dx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3157                   dy = -\/dy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3158                   t = x0, x0 = xb, xb = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3159                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3160                \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(dy >= 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3161                \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(dx >= 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3162 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3163                x1 = (int) x\_top;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3164                x2 = (int) x\_bottom;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3165                \textcolor{comment}{// compute intersection with y axis at x1+1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3166                y\_crossing = y\_top + dy * (x1+1 -\/ x0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3167 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3168                \textcolor{comment}{// compute intersection with y axis at x2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3169                y\_final = y\_top + dy * (x2 -\/ x0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3170 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3171                \textcolor{comment}{//           x1    x\_top                            x2    x\_bottom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3172                \textcolor{comment}{//     y\_top  +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/|-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3173                \textcolor{comment}{//            |            |            |            |            |            |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3174                \textcolor{comment}{//            |            |            |            |            |            |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3175                \textcolor{comment}{//       sy0  |      Txxxxx|............|............|............|............|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3176                \textcolor{comment}{// y\_crossing |            *xxxxx.......|............|............|............|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3177                \textcolor{comment}{//            |            |     xxxxx..|............|............|............|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3178                \textcolor{comment}{//            |            |     /-\/   xx*xxxx........|............|............|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3179                \textcolor{comment}{//            |            | dy <       |    xxxxxx..|............|............|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3180                \textcolor{comment}{//   y\_final  |            |     \(\backslash\)-\/     |          xx*xxx.........|............|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3181                \textcolor{comment}{//       sy1  |            |            |            |   xxxxxB...|............|}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3182                \textcolor{comment}{//            |            |            |            |            |            |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3183                \textcolor{comment}{//            |            |            |            |            |            |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3184                \textcolor{comment}{//  y\_bottom  +-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3185                \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3186                \textcolor{comment}{// goal is to measure the area covered by '.' in each pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3187 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3188                \textcolor{comment}{// if x2 is right at the right edge of x1, y\_crossing can blow up, github \#1057}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3189                \textcolor{comment}{// @TODO: maybe test against sy1 rather than y\_bottom?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3190                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (y\_crossing > y\_bottom)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3191                   y\_crossing = y\_bottom;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3192 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3193                sign = e-\/>direction;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3194 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3195                \textcolor{comment}{// area of the rectangle covered from sy0..y\_crossing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3196                area = sign * (y\_crossing-\/sy0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3197 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3198                \textcolor{comment}{// area of the triangle (x\_top,sy0), (x1+1,sy0), (x1+1,y\_crossing)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3199                scanline[x1] += stbtt\_\_sized\_triangle\_area(area, x1+1 -\/ x\_top);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3200 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3201                \textcolor{comment}{// check if final y\_crossing is blown up; no test case for this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3202                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (y\_final > y\_bottom) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3203                   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} denom = (x2 -\/ (x1+1));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3204                   y\_final = y\_bottom;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3205                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (denom != 0) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// [DEAR IMGUI] Avoid div by zero (https://github.com/nothings/stb/issues/1316)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3206                      dy = (y\_final -\/ y\_crossing ) / denom; \textcolor{comment}{// if denom=0, y\_final = y\_crossing, so y\_final <= y\_bottom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3207                   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3208                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3209 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3210                \textcolor{comment}{// in second pixel, area covered by line segment found in first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3211                \textcolor{comment}{// is always a rectangle 1 wide * the height of that line segment; this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3212                \textcolor{comment}{// is exactly what the variable 'area' stores. it also gets a contribution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3213                \textcolor{comment}{// from the line segment within it. the THIRD pixel will get the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3214                \textcolor{comment}{// pixel's rectangle contribution, the second pixel's rectangle contribution,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3215                \textcolor{comment}{// and its own contribution. the 'own contribution' is the same in every pixel except}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3216                \textcolor{comment}{// the leftmost and rightmost, a trapezoid that slides down in each pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3217                \textcolor{comment}{// the second pixel's contribution to the third pixel will be the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3218                \textcolor{comment}{// rectangle 1 wide times the height change in the second pixel, which is dy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3219 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3220                step = sign * dy * 1; \textcolor{comment}{// dy is dy/dx, change in y for every 1 change in x,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3221                \textcolor{comment}{// which multiplied by 1-\/pixel-\/width is how much pixel area changes for each step in x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3222                \textcolor{comment}{// so the area advances by 'step' every time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3223 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3224                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (x = x1+1; x < x2; ++x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3225                   scanline[x] += area + step/2; \textcolor{comment}{// area of trapezoid is 1*step/2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3226                   area += step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3227                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3228                \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a2b639a5c1ed39bb9e223a78b743f3769}{STBTT\_fabs}}(area) <= 1.01f); \textcolor{comment}{// accumulated error from area += step unless we round step down}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3229                \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_a1123d905f512c19c8d796a6d294a3a84}{STBTT\_assert}}(sy1 > y\_final-\/0.01f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3230 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3231                \textcolor{comment}{// area covered in the last pixel is the rectangle from all the pixels to the left,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3232                \textcolor{comment}{// plus the trapezoid filled by the line segment in this pixel all the way to the right edge}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3233                scanline[x2] += area + sign * stbtt\_\_position\_trapezoid\_area(sy1-\/y\_final, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}) x2, x2+1.0f, x\_bottom, x2+1.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3234 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3235                \textcolor{comment}{// the rest of the line is filled based on the total height of the line segment in this pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3236                scanline\_fill[x2] += sign * (sy1-\/sy0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3237             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3238          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3239             \textcolor{comment}{// if edge goes outside of box we're drawing, we require}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3240             \textcolor{comment}{// clipping logic. since this does not match the intended use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3241             \textcolor{comment}{// of this library, we use a different, very slow brute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3242             \textcolor{comment}{// force implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3243             \textcolor{comment}{// note though that this does happen some of the time because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3244             \textcolor{comment}{// x\_top and x\_bottom can be extrapolated at the top \& bottom of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3245             \textcolor{comment}{// the shape and actually lie outside the bounding box}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3246             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3247             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (x=0; x < len; ++x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3248                \textcolor{comment}{// cases:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3249                \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3250                \textcolor{comment}{// there can be up to two intersections with the pixel. any intersection}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3251                \textcolor{comment}{// with left or right edges can be handled by splitting into two (or three)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3252                \textcolor{comment}{// regions. intersections with top \& bottom do not necessitate case-\/wise logic.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253                \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254                \textcolor{comment}{// the old way of doing this found the intersections with the left \& right edges,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3255                \textcolor{comment}{// then used some simple logic to produce up to three segments in sorted order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256                \textcolor{comment}{// from top-\/to-\/bottom. however, this had a problem: if an x edge was epsilon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3257                \textcolor{comment}{// across the x border, then the corresponding y position might not be distinct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258                \textcolor{comment}{// from the other y segment, and it might ignored as an empty segment. to avoid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3259                \textcolor{comment}{// that, we need to explicitly produce segments based on x positions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3261                \textcolor{comment}{// rename variables to clearly-\/defined pairs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3262                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y0 = y\_top;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x1 = (float) (x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3264                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x2 = (float) (x+1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3265                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x3 = xb;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y3 = y\_bottom;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3267 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3268                \textcolor{comment}{// x = e-\/>x + e-\/>dx * (y-\/y\_top)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269                \textcolor{comment}{// (y-\/y\_top) = (x -\/ e-\/>x) / e-\/>dx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270                \textcolor{comment}{// y = (x -\/ e-\/>x) / e-\/>dx + y\_top}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3271                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y1 = (x -\/ x0) / dx + y\_top;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y2 = (x+1 -\/ x0) / dx + y\_top;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3273 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3274                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 < x1 \&\& x3 > x2) \{         \textcolor{comment}{// three segments descending down-\/right}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x0,y0, x1,y1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x1,y1, x2,y2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x2,y2, x3,y3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x3 < x1 \&\& x0 > x2) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// three segments descending down-\/left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x0,y0, x2,y2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x2,y2, x1,y1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3281                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x1,y1, x3,y3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3282                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 < x1 \&\& x3 > x1) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// two segments across x, down-\/right}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3283                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x0,y0, x1,y1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3284                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x1,y1, x3,y3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3285                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x3 < x1 \&\& x0 > x1) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// two segments across x, down-\/left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3286                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x0,y0, x1,y1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3287                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x1,y1, x3,y3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3288                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x0 < x2 \&\& x3 > x2) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// two segments across x+1, down-\/right}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3289                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x0,y0, x2,y2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3290                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x2,y2, x3,y3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3291                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x3 < x2 \&\& x0 > x2) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// two segments across x+1, down-\/left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3292                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x0,y0, x2,y2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3293                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x2,y2, x3,y3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3294                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{  \textcolor{comment}{// one segment}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3295                   stbtt\_\_handle\_clipped\_edge(scanline,x,e, x0,y0, x3,y3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3296                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3297             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3298          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3299       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3300       e = e-\/>next;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3301    \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3425 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbtt\_\_sort\_edges\_quicksort(stbtt\_\_edge *p, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3426 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3427    \textcolor{comment}{/* threshold for transitioning to insertion sort */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3428    \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (n > 12) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3429       stbtt\_\_edge t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3430       \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c01,c12,c,m,i,j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3431 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3432       \textcolor{comment}{/* compute median of three */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433       m = n >> 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434       c01 = STBTT\_\_COMPARE(\&p[0],\&p[m]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3435       c12 = STBTT\_\_COMPARE(\&p[m],\&p[n-\/1]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436       \textcolor{comment}{/* if 0 >= mid >= end, or 0 < mid < end, then use mid */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c01 != c12) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438          \textcolor{comment}{/* otherwise, we'll need to swap something else to middle */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440          c = STBTT\_\_COMPARE(\&p[0],\&p[n-\/1]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441          \textcolor{comment}{/* 0>mid \&\& mid<n:  0>n => n; 0<n => 0 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442          \textcolor{comment}{/* 0<mid \&\& mid>n:  0>n => 0; 0<n => n */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443          z = (c == c12) ? 0 : n-\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444          t = p[z];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3445          p[z] = p[m];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446          p[m] = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3448       \textcolor{comment}{/* now p[m] is the median-\/of-\/three */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449       \textcolor{comment}{/* swap it to the beginning so it won't move around */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450       t = p[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451       p[0] = p[m];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452       p[m] = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3453 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3454       \textcolor{comment}{/* partition loop */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455       i=1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3456       j=n-\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(;;) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458          \textcolor{comment}{/* handling of equality is crucial here */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459          \textcolor{comment}{/* for sentinels \& efficiency with duplicates */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3460          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (;;++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3461             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!STBTT\_\_COMPARE(\&p[i], \&p[0])) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (;;-\/-\/j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!STBTT\_\_COMPARE(\&p[0], \&p[j])) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466          \textcolor{comment}{/* make sure we haven't crossed */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i >= j) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468          t = p[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469          p[i] = p[j];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470          p[j] = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3471 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3472          ++i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473          -\/-\/j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3474       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475       \textcolor{comment}{/* recurse on smaller side, iterate on larger */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j < (n-\/i)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477          stbtt\_\_sort\_edges\_quicksort(p,j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478          p = p+i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479          n = n-\/i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481          stbtt\_\_sort\_edges\_quicksort(p+i, n-\/i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482          n = j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3485 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3527          \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a=k,b=j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3528          \textcolor{comment}{// skip the edge if horizontal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3529          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (p[j].y == p[k].y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3530             \textcolor{keywordflow}{continue};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3531          \textcolor{comment}{// add edge from j to k to the list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3532          e[n].invert = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3533          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (invert ? p[j].y > p[k].y : p[j].y < p[k].y) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3534             e[n].invert = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3535             a=j,b=k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3536          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3537          e[n].x0 = p[a].x * scale\_x + shift\_x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3538          e[n].y0 = (p[a].y * y\_scale\_inv + shift\_y) * vsubsample;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3539          e[n].x1 = p[b].x * scale\_x + shift\_x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3540          e[n].y1 = (p[b].y * y\_scale\_inv + shift\_y) * vsubsample;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3541          ++n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3542       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3543    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3544 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3547    stbtt\_\_sort\_edges(e, n);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4024    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} j;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4029       STBTT\_memset(buffer, 0, kernel\_width);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4030 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4031       total = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4032 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4033       \textcolor{comment}{// make kernel\_width a constant in common cases so compiler can optimize out the divide}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4034       \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (kernel\_width) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4035          \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 2:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4036             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i <= safe\_w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4037                total += pixels[i] -\/ buffer[i \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4038                buffer[(i+kernel\_width) \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK] = pixels[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4039                pixels[i] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char) (total / 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4040             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4041             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4042          \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 3:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4043             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i <= safe\_w; ++i) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4046                pixels[i] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char) (total / 3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4047             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4048             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4049          \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 4:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4050             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i <= safe\_w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4051                total += pixels[i] -\/ buffer[i \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4052                buffer[(i+kernel\_width) \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK] = pixels[i];}

\DoxyCodeLine{4054             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4055             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4056          \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 5:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4057             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i <= safe\_w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4058                total += pixels[i] -\/ buffer[i \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4059                buffer[(i+kernel\_width) \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK] = pixels[i];}

\DoxyCodeLine{4065                total += pixels[i] -\/ buffer[i \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4066                buffer[(i+kernel\_width) \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK] = pixels[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4067                pixels[i] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char) (total / kernel\_width);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4068             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4069             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4070       \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4074          total -\/= buffer[i \& STBTT\_\_OVER\_MASK];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4075          pixels[i] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char) (total / kernel\_width);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4076       \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4406 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbtt\_\_ray\_intersect\_bezier(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} orig[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ray[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q0[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q1[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q2[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} hits[2][2])}
\DoxyCodeLine{4407 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4408    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q0perp = q0[1]*ray[0] -\/ q0[0]*ray[1];}

\DoxyCodeLine{4413    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = q0perp -\/ 2*q1perp + q2perp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4414    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} b = q1perp -\/ q0perp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4415    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} c = q0perp -\/ roperp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4416 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4417    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} s0 = 0., s1 = 0.;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4418    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} num\_s = 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4422       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (discr > 0.0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4423          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} rcpna = -\/1 / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4424          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} d = (float) \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__draw_8cpp_ace1fcbebd394a5bed76bc9b97dbe8d5a}{STBTT\_sqrt}}(discr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4425          s0 = (b+d) * rcpna;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4426          s1 = (b-\/d) * rcpna;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4427          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s0 >= 0.0 \&\& s0 <= 1.0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4428             num\_s = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4429          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (d > 0.0 \&\& s1 >= 0.0 \&\& s1 <= 1.0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4430             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (num\_s == 0) s0 = s1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4431             ++num\_s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4432          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4433       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4434    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4435       \textcolor{comment}{// 2*b*s + c = 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4436       \textcolor{comment}{// s = -\/c / (2*b)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4437       s0 = c / (-\/2 * b);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4438       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s0 >= 0.0 \&\& s0 <= 1.0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4439          num\_s = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4440    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4441 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4442    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (num\_s == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4443       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4444    \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4445       \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} rcp\_len2 = 1 / (ray[0]*ray[0] + ray[1]*ray[1]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4446       \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} rayn\_x = ray[0] * rcp\_len2, rayn\_y = ray[1] * rcp\_len2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4447 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4450       \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q2d =   q2[0]*rayn\_x +   q2[1]*rayn\_y;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4458       hits[0][1] = a*s0+b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4459 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4460       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (num\_s > 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4461          hits[1][0] = q0rd + s1*(2.0f -\/ 2.0f*s1)*q10d + s1*s1*q20d;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4462          hits[1][1] = a*s1+b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4463          \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4464       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4465          \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4466       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4467    \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4783 \textcolor{comment}{// check if a utf8 string contains a prefix which is the utf16 string; if so return length of matching utf8 string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4784 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbtt\_int32 stbtt\_\_CompareUTF8toUTF16\_bigendian\_prefix(stbtt\_uint8 *s1, stbtt\_int32 len1, stbtt\_uint8 *s2, stbtt\_int32 len2)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4786    stbtt\_int32 i=0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4787 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4788    \textcolor{comment}{// convert utf16 to utf8 and compare the results while converting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4789    \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len2) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4790       stbtt\_uint16 ch = s2[0]*256 + s2[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4791       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ch < 0x80) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4792          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i >= len1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4793          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s1[i++] != ch) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4794       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ch < 0x800) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4795          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i+1 >= len1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4796          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s1[i++] != 0xc0 + (ch >> 6)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4797          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s1[i++] != 0x80 + (ch \& 0x3f)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4798       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ch >= 0xd800 \&\& ch < 0xdc00) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4799          stbtt\_uint32 c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4800          stbtt\_uint16 ch2 = s2[2]*256 + s2[3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4801          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i+3 >= len1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4802          c = ((ch -\/ 0xd800) << 10) + (ch2 -\/ 0xdc00) + 0x10000;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4803          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s1[i++] != 0xf0 + (c >> 18)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4804          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s1[i++] != 0x80 + ((c >> 12) \& 0x3f)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4805          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s1[i++] != 0x80 + ((c >>  6) \& 0x3f)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4806          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s1[i++] != 0x80 + ((c      ) \& 0x3f)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4807          s2 += 2; \textcolor{comment}{// plus another 2 below}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4808          len2 -\/= 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4809       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ch >= 0xdc00 \&\& ch < 0xe000) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4811       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4812          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i+2 >= len1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
